< review>
Those with food allergies, beware- you will likely be refused service.

I came in on my birthday to get my birthday buy one get one free ice cream. I have a nut allergy, but my personal comfort level is that as long as basic precautions are taken (clean scoop, gloves, mixing surface, ice cream from the back or an untouched area of the tin), I am ok at eating at places that could have cross contact. I have eaten at numerous other Cold Stone locations that have happily accommodates these requests.

The employee working that day seemed completely clueless as to the birthday club reward, and refused to serve me because of my allergies. He stated that it was because he didn't know how other employees used the utensils, which is fair. However, rinsing them one final time would have remedied this situation, and avoided my disappointment and humiliation.

I even stated that I do not expect them by any means to guarantee that my ice cream would not have any traces of nuts. I understand that he was trying to refuse service for my safety, however, I am an adult and able to make these decisions for myself.</review>

Maaco Lake Forest Cal.  OUTSTANDING
I read a lot of reviews on the internet in search of an inexpensive paint job for my 12 year-old Dodge Dakota that I had left out in the elements its entire life.  The paint was in such bad shape that it was actually peeling and cracked down to the metal.  I mostly read poor reviews for other Maaco franchises but the one in Lake Forest got a number of good reviews.  Turns out that all Maaco paint and body shops do not turn out the same quality of work.  I was on a budget and didn‚Äôt want to spend $3000 to $3600, which I was quoted at other body shops, on and old ‚ÄúJunker‚Äù truck.  Not expecting too much I brought the truck to Peter & Miguel at Maaco in Lake Forest.  (Oh did I mention that I wanted to change the color from a lousy dark blue to an ‚ÄúAlpine‚Äù white?)  Well Peter, Miguel and their crew FAR EXCEEDED MY EXPECTIONS.  I was blown away when I got my truck back.  It looked brand new!  The pulled the bed away from the cab and painted the space in between.  They sanded, prepped and primed the rest of the truck prior to shooting and the finished job had not a hint of orange peel and no runs anywhere.  They even painted the door jambs.  Let me say the paint came out smooth as silk and would be hard to tell from an original factory paint job.  Now, let me state:  I am not being paid or compensated in any way for writing this review.  In fact I don‚Äôt know if Peter and Miguel even know I‚Äôm writing it.  I just think someone who performs a great service at a more than fair price should get a good review.  (Lord knows that there are too many people out there that don‚Äôt want to pay for decent job and than are quick to write a bad review.)  So, to say that I‚Äôm happy with their work would be an understatement.  And I would whole heartedly recommend this franchise to my friends and relatives.  BTW the whole thing including some extras I wanted came to $1,406 OTD.  That turns out to be $2,094 that a didn‚Äôt have to spend.  LOVE IT!

I walked into this shop as a beginner, looking for specific, overly advanced card manipulation books (mentioned by world-class experts like Michael Vincent in talks I'd seen on the web). Joe recognized this and strongly suggested that I start out with other, more beginner-friendly material. Months later, I couldn't be happier that I took his recommendations. <name>Shanelle S< /name><Time>1589749873585< /Time><Rate>5</Rate><Text>Taiwanese spot known for their crispy ‚Äúchar siu‚Äù pork (red grain pork). My sister raves about this place for its plentiful serving size, delicious food, and reasonable prices. We were glad to see that they‚Äôre still operating during covid, and when we called in, said they were open from 11am-8pm. They offer takeout and there‚Äôs free parking since it‚Äôs located in the Diamond Plaza. Their A2 red grain pork with rice is a popular option and good for a first time visitor. The texture of the pork (especially the end piece) is so crispy and succulent. I liked that they mix browned pork with the rice and provide saut√©ed cabbage and pickled veggies on the side. I personally prefer the red grain pork with the dry noodle (C1) although I definitely recommend mixing it well since all the sauce drops to the bottom. The noodles were perfectly chewy and there was a generous amount of bean sprouts. We got an order of popcorn chicken and they made it fresh. I like that it‚Äôs not overly salted like at TenRen. Also got the Hokkaido milk tea with boba which was a good size and had the right amount of sweetness/creaminess. After we called in the order the food was ready in 15 min. They do take credit card. We fed a family of four for ~$32 which was a great deal. Overall a yummy option for when you‚Äôre hungry and are craving some Taiwanese food.< /Text>< Pictures>

<Rating>4<//Rating><Review>Start off with the BBQ Pork Special (item #1). At quick glance, it resembles Cantonese char siu, but that's where the similarities end. Slightly fried on the outside to give it a light crunch, juicy and tender on the inside, and all while maintaining a perfect BBQ flavor. The combination comes with a tasty minced meat rice and a vegetable. Add an egg and it'd be just like those Taiwanese lunch boxes.

The restaurant is small, and the biggest table seats 4, so don't roll up with your entire Monja entourage. TV could be put to better use, rather than cycling through pictures of Taiwan night markets, Wanhua and Monga the film, but hey, who am I to complain about pictures of Ethan Yuan!

Will have to be back to try the rest of the menu, including the chicken roll and their homemade sausages!

Mini back story: The new owner/chef is actually from the Wanhua region in Taipei, and learned the art of BBQ pork from a 3-generation restaurant.<//Review><pictures>None</pictures><Response>None</Response><gmap_id>0x80c32a5dc990d163:0x670b341eaf42bfc7< /gmap_id></record>

< text>
I love this place!!!  It's clean,  quaint and the staff are super nice.  Some people have commented that it's dated. It's clean!  Nothing in our room was torn or tattered.
It's charming!!!  I love that is not trendy. It made my vacation seem like a get away.  The property and rooms are well maintained! Some people commented on the sound proofing and being woken up. <rating>5</rating>< review>
My first time here and it definitely won't be my last. I got the avocado & quinoa salad to-go and it was the best salad I've ever had in my life. Super filling, amazing flavors, and a nice little crunch too! I was trying to decide between this salad and the sophisticated salad. The super friendly cashier helped me decide on the avocado salad. She said both were great, but the avocado was the most popular salad and a safer choice, where as the sophisticated salad is more complex. Long story short, I went with the avocado and loved it.

All of the staff I interacted with were so friendly and welcoming. Everyone had a smile on their face and looked genuinely happy to be there.

If you haven't been to Mendocino Farms, GO! & if you haven't tried the avocado & quinoa salad, GET IT!< /review>

Modern farmhouse design and seating, great tasting healthy happy food in the middle of studio City! Awesome. Stop by and check it out. This is worth the stop for food. Not pricey as one might expect. They have a section for kids to sit if they want to play on there own. I like they have filtered water versus tap. I chose the chicken cobb salad with the dressing mixed in while my wife went with the turkey club on a pretzel roll. The taste was amazing. I was truly impressed.<//Text>

We were excited to try Mendocino Farms and found it to be a great newish place with an enthusiastic and friendly staff, and lots of vegetarian, vegan, and gluten-free options.

I had the blue plate special which was half a sandwich and my choice of sides. I had a caprese sandwich which was delicious and very fresh tasting, along with the beet and quinoa side, which was also great and included chunks of green apples (which were a delightful surprise.)

Our kid really enjoyed his grilled cheese sandwich (but he refused to eat the side of apples out of some kind of crazy kid-based non-sensical principle.)

My wife had the Vegan Green Goddess Avocado toast on gluten-free bread. She thought it was good, albeit perhaps a little too much was going on in the dish, so it was hard to identify specifically what was great about it. (It‚Äôs also possible she just wasn‚Äôt in the mood to offer too much of an assessment to further my agenda of being a crazy prolific reviews writer.)

This location offers both Inside and outside seating and it was very crowded on our Sunday afternoon visit, so we had trouble finding the table and ended up crowding together at a table for two. Ultimately this is the sign of a restaurant whose food is worth the visit.

We‚Äôll definitely be back to try the many options available to us with out family‚Äôs various vegetarian, gluten free, and kid-centric diets.< /text>

<rating>4<//rating>< text>
The only reason why this place is not getting 5 start is because i feel their food isn't as consistently tasty as I'd like it to be.

Been to this location a few times now. They are always packed! Their sandwiches are always delicious. Sides for me are a hit or miss but overall, pretty decent. I haven't had a salad / soup here but I am interested to see what they are all about.The best part about Mendocino Farms is their variety. They have something for everyone. I will say, each of the menu items I have had are always well thought out. The flavor profiles of the ingredients pair well together, always.

The atmosphere of the restaurant is more modern with a variety of dining options. They do have some games and entertainment for kids / adults to enjoy while they eat and wait. There's always a buzzing, high energy you can look forward to. If you want to stay out of the hustle and bustle, take a seat outside! It's a nice, relaxing change from inside.

If you haven't tried it, I would absolutely give it a shot! It's worth it for a well made sandwich.<//text>

I wanted to take by buyer client out for lunch. We come here a lot and it's always consistently good. My favorite sandwich is the chicken-prosciutto sandwich, which had a pesto-like sauce. < Text>
sandwiches here are tasty and solid.  i always end up going for the pork belly banh mi.  very flavorful and a good lunch size.  the vegetables are crunchy and fresh, and the pork belly is cooked well with good seasoning or marinade.  the panini bread could be a little hotter but that‚Äôs a niggle.

deduct one star for their setup which is an efficiency nightmare.  a person stands at the entrance and takes your order and has to go into excruciating detail explaining the ingredients in the sandwich (which are listed right in front of you) and then you walk down a ramp to pay.

except they have a stand/mini-deli counter setup with their sides and another person asking if you want to try free samples.  which holds up the payment process.

love the food but call ahead and order and skip the line and pick up your food at the other end so you can avoid the dissertation on the ingredients and the sample counter.

oh, and most of the time the person finishing your order at the phone order side will give you the soda for free.< /Text>

<userid>102761999783078995895<//userid><Name>Samantha Sanchez</Name><time>1524628468011</time><rating>5<//rating><text>My boss orders salads for delivery all the time and raves about this place. OKAY, now I get it.  The place was super busy and packed, but seating was available.  Ranged from people on there lunch breaks, seasoned citizens to a group of moms each with their baby strollers trying to manuever through the dining area.

Since this was my first time here, i wasn't really sure what to get.  They offer a seasonal menu, along with their classics and favorites, as well as vegan options.

It's set up cafeteria style and you order with the hostess.  I asked for a recommendation and the hostess suggested the Peruvian Steak Sandwich.  I was concerned it would be smothered in cheese, so she suggested light cheese.

Near the cashier counter they have fresh made deli items, like pastas and slaws that you can sample.  As I passed down the line you can see all the food being prepared and I noticed some delicious looking bacon bits.

We met Matt, the manager in training.  He came over to say hello and asked if we needed anything, so we asked if we could have a sample of that bacon?  Not only did he give us the bacon bits, but he also gave a us a little taste of some mouth watering make you wanna slap your momma Pork Belly!!  SO GOOD!

The hostess was spot on about my sandwich!! It was so tasty,  you'll see in my pix what's left of my sandwich when I finally remembered to snap a shot.

My co-worker ordered the Modern Tuna "Almost Melt" sandwich with dill pickle potato chips.  I'm purdy sure the sandwich was really good since she wouldn't let the staff take her finished plate because she wanted to eat every crumb and for a second I thought she was going to lick the serving tray to get every morsel of food.

I noticed after that they have a Blue Plate Special which I'm excited to go back to experience other items.  I'll keep you posted of what I discover.

Enjoy!<//text>< pics>

<Review>This place has decent food, but the dumbest system I have seen in a long time.  If you are putting in a to go order or any order for that matter, you put it in with hostess. So the line is out the door and the small entry way is crowded with people. Then you move to another counter where you pay, but here yyou can try different salads to add to your order. So now the two employees behind that counter are trying to take money and give you samples. Nowncones the wait for your to go order.  I waited half an hour for one sandwich.  Lesson learned, always pre order for quickest in and out.  Staff is friendly.  Atmosphere us nice. Food is tasty. But what a crappy time.</Review>< username>
